op{constructor(e,t={}){this.retryPolicy=e,this.logger=t.logger,this.enableRequestLogging=t.enableRequestLogging??!0,this.enablePerformanceTracking=t.enablePerformanceTracking??!0}async execute(e){const t=await this.executeWithResult(e);if(t.success)return t.data;throw t.error||new Error("Request failed without specific error")}async executeWithResult(e){const t=Date.now(),i=[];let n,o=0;for(this.logRequestStart(e);;){o++;const s=new Date,r=1===o?0:this.retryPolicy.calculateDelay(o-1,n);r>0&&(this.logger?.debug({requestId:e.id,attemptNumber:o,delayMs:r},"Waiting before retry error occurred","unknown")}sleep(e){return new request")}logRequestSuccess(e,t,i){this.enableRequestLogging&&this.logger&&this.logger.info({requestId:e.id,totalAttempts:t,totalTimeMs:i,retriesNeeded:t-1},"Retryable request completed successfully")}logRequestFailure(e,t,i,n){this.logger&&this.logger.error({requestId:e.id,totalAttempts:t,totalTimeMs:i,finalError:n.toObject()},"Retryable request failed after all attempts")}logRetryAttempt(e,t,i){this.enableRequestLogging&&this.logger&&this.logger.warn({requestId:e.id,attemptNumber:t,error:i.toObject()},"Request attempt failed, will
